	title = korea.86.title
	desc = korea.86.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_86
	
	fire_only_once = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = korea.86.a
		KOR = {
			country_event = {
				id = korea.87
				days = 5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_everything_so_good_tt
			1066 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			989 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			529 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_0
				amount = 3500
				producer = USA
			}

			add_offsite_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
			}
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 2
			}
			JAP = {
				set_portraits = {
					character = JAP_emperor_hirohito
					civilian = { 
						large ="gfx/leaders/JAP/Portrait_JAP_showa_hirohito_2.png"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = { 
	id = korea.87
	title = korea.87.title
	desc = korea.87.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_86
	
	fire_only_once = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = korea.87.a
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JAP
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					TBJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = TBJ
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					SDJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = SDJ
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					NBJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = NBJ
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					FJP = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = FJP
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					GJJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = GJJ
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}	
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = JAP
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = KOR
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = KOR
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = japan.1116
					days = 4
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					USA = {
						has_war_with = KOR
					}
				}
				JAP = {
					add_to_faction = USA
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = korea.89
	title = korea.89.title
	desc = korea.89.desc
	picture = GFX_TLE_korea_event_none
	
	fire_only_once = yes	
	trigger = {
			has_country_flag = FLAG_USA_FUCK_TO_KOREA
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = FLAG_SAY_SORRY_TO_USA
			}
			not = {
				has_decision = KOR_not_say_the_panay
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = KOR_KILL_NOSESE
			}
			always = no
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 50
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = korea.89.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TOOLTIP_IT_WILL_BE_DISASTER_MOON
			set_country_flag = KOR_KILL_NOSESE
			hidden_effect = {
				USA = {
					country_event = {
						id = korea.69
						days = 2
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
						OR = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							NOT = {
								owner = {
									any_owned_state = {
										free_building_slots = {
											building = arms_factory
											size > 0
											include_locked = yes
										}
										is_in_home_area = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
						OR = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							NOT = {
								owner = {
									any_owned_state = {
										free_building_slots = {
											building = arms_factory
											size > 0
											include_locked = yes
										}
										is_in_home_area = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = industrial_complex
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
						OR = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							NOT = {
								owner = {
									any_owned_state = {
										free_building_slots = {
											building = industrial_complex
											size > 0
											include_locked = yes
										}
										is_in_home_area = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = industrial_complex
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
						OR = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							NOT = {
								owner = {
									any_owned_state = {
										free_building_slots = {
											building = industrial_complex
											size > 0
											include_locked = yes
										}
										is_in_home_area = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.89.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TOOLTIP_TLE_ENDING_BAD
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = KOR
			}
			white_peace = KOR
			create_wargoal = {
				target = KOR
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			ideology = fascism
			size = 0.65
			capital = 525
			states = { 
				527 1017 1019 1025 1023 1026 1024
			}
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			Character = KOR_emperor_yi_jin
			country_leader = {
				#expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				desc="KOR_yi_jin_desc"
				traits = {
					korea_emperor
				}
			}
			promote_leader = yes
		}	
		set_capital = { state = 525 }
	}
}

	}

				transfer_troops = no

				target = SHX
				transfer_troops = no

				target = SZC
				transfer_troops = no
			}

				target = XSM
				transfer_troops = no
			}

			}

			}
			annex_country = {
				target = YUN
				transfer_troops = no
			}

			}

	id = korea.105 #중국이 항복한다 하였노라.

	picture = GFX_TLE_korea_event_none

	option = { #승리다!
		name = korea.105.a
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				KOR = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = FLAG_EVENT_251_A
						has_country_flag = FLAG_EVENT_251_B
					}
				}
			}
		}	
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = FLAG_EVENT_251_A
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TOOLTIP_EVENT_KOREA_105_A
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = FLAG_EVENT_251_B
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TOOLTIP_EVENT_KOREA_105_B
		}
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			country_event = {
				id = korea.106
				days = 3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_political_power = 100
			SOV = {
				add_ideas = SOV_none_attack_korea
			}
			KOR = {
				add_ideas = KOR_none_attack_soviert
			}
			country_event = {
				id = korea.166
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = korea.105.b
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				KOR = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = FLAG_EVENT_251_A
						has_country_flag = FLAG_EVENT_251_B
					}
				}
			}
		}	
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = korea.107
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = korea.244 #서려혁전 준비
	title = korea.244.title
	desc = korea.244.desc
	picture = GFX_TLE_korea_event_none
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #끝까지 간다!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		name = korea.244.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.1
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.244.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
			white_peace = SOV
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = SOV_TNO
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = NV1
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = KAZ
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					NOT = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = SOV_TNO
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				target = NV1
				type = annex_everything
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				target = KAZ
				type = annex_everything
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				target = YN1
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = TMS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = BY1
			type = annex_everything
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = RUS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = FIN
			type = annex_everything
		}
		SOV = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = SOV
			remove_ideas = TLE_afterwar_idea
			set_capital = { state = 219 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = korea.300 #강명제 친정선언

	desc = korea.300.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_300
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = korea.300.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = EVENT_KOREA_300_TOOLTIP
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = KOR_Weakening_the_kingship
			set_country_flag = FLAG_KOR_DEMOCRACY_ROUTE
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			complete_national_focus = KOR_the_democracy_route
			news_event = { id = eok_news.49 days = 1 }
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				character = KOR_kim_hui_sun
				ideology = korean_democracy
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				last_election = "1932.9.23"
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				Character = KOR_emperor_yi_jin
				country_leader = {
					#expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = despotism
					desc="YI_CHIN_DESC"
					traits = {
						korea_emperor
					}
				}
				promote_leader = yes
			}	
			add_country_leader_role = {
				Character = KOR_emperor_yi_jin
				country_leader = {
					#expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = korean_democracy
					desc="YI_CHIN_DESC"
					traits = {
						korea_emperor
					}
				}
				promote_leader = yes
			}	
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = "KOR_emperor_ruling_party"
				name = "KOR_emperor_ruling_party"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = "KOR_hwangguk_party_long"
				name = "KOR_hwangguk_party"
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_event_korea_351
	
    is_triggered_only = yes

		MEN_attack_start_mongol_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { #그래 시작해보자고
		name = korea.351.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		KOR = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MON
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			MEN = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = MON
					type = annex_everything
				}
				load_oob = "KOR_MEN"
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = MON
				}
				add_core_of = MEN
			}
		}
	}
}

				has_country_flag = TLE_KOR_WIN_IN_CHINA_FUCKYEAH

				rule = TLE_KOR_GREAT_RULE

			}

		}

			NOT = {

			}

		date > 1945.8.15
	}

			GER = {
				set_technology = {
					nukes = 1
				}
			}
		}

		KOR = {

			has_war_with = USA
		}
		is_historical_focus_on = yes
		OR = {
			KOR = {
				has_completed_focus = KOR_baekje_kisadan
			}
			has_game_rule = {
				rule = TLE_KOR_GREAT_RULE
				option = TLE_KOR_GREAT_RULE_WIN
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = FLAG_TLE_KOR_GREAT_SETTING
		}
		date > 1946.1.4
	}				
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			629 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			USA = {
				transfer_state = 629
			}
			KOR = {
				set_country_flag = FLAG_TLE_KOR_GREAT_SETTING
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #그래 시작해보자고
		name = korea.360.a
		launch_nuke = {

country_event = { #
	id = korea.1114
	title = korea.1114.title
	desc = korea.1114.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_1114
	
    is_triggered_only = yes
	 
	option = { #
		name = korea.1114.a
		set_global_flag = TLE_PAK_JAP_ATTACK
		custom_effect_tooltip = TLE_EVENT_KOREA_1114
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JAP
			type = annex_everything 
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					KKS = {
						exists = yes
						is_puppet_of = KOR
					}
				}
				KKS = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = JAP
						type = annex_everything 
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NBJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				add_to_faction = NBJ
				NBJ = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = JAP
						type = annex_everything 
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SDJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				add_to_faction = SDJ
				SDJ = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = JAP
						type = annex_everything 
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					TBJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				add_to_faction = TBJ
				TBJ = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = JAP
						type = annex_everything 
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	hidden = yes

				has_global_flag = GLOB_PCY_KUOMINTANG_COLLAPSED_1
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {

					has_state_flag = hubei_province_state
					has_state_flag = henan_province_state
					has_state_flag = zhejiang_province_state
				}
				is_owned_by = CHI
			}

		}

		}

				set_autonomy = { target = DK2 autonomy_state = korean_bunguk }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = DKG
				}
				add_core_of = DK2
			}
			DK2 = {
				transfer_state = 1064
				transfer_state = 1068
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					last_election = "1936.3.15"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 0
					fascism = 0
					communism = 0
					neutrality = 100
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						KOR = {
							has_country_flag = KOR_dec_jap_trainning_support_flag
						}
					}
					load_oob = "DK2_nasang_kks"
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NBJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				DK2 = {
					annex_country = {
						target = NBJ
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SDJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				DK2 = {
					annex_country = {
						target = SDJ
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					TBJ = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				DK2 = {
					annex_country = {
						target = TBJ
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = JAP
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}	
			KHK = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = JAP
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			DK2 = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = JAP
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			1068 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #혁명일심회
	id = korea.2700
	title = korea.2700.title
	desc = korea.2700.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_2700
	
    is_triggered_only = yes
	 
	option = { #한국
		name = korea.2700.a
		KKS_KCS_coupdetat_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			716 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}	
			328 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}	
			717 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}	
			408 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}	
			409 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}	
			1029 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}	
			set_country_flag = FLAG_BOP_KOR_DONE
			set_power_balance = {
				id = KOR_balance
				left_side = KOR_the_emperor
				right_side = KOR_millitary
				set_default = yes 
				set_value = -0.55
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = korea.2703
	title = korea.2703.title
	desc = korea.2703.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_2703
	
    is_triggered_only = yes
	 
	option = { #한국
		name = korea.2703.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_character_name = {
				character = KOR_kim_koo
				name = "KOR_kim_koo"
			}
			set_variable = { sinhan_party = 0 }
			set_variable = { social_party = 0 }
			set_variable = { democratic_party = 0 }
			set_variable = { korea_party = 0 }
			set_variable = { imperial_party = 0 }
			set_variable = { national_revouliton_party = 500 }
			set_variable = { korean_resistance_party = 0 }
			set_variable = { communist_party = 0 }
			set_variable = { independent_party = 0 }
			set_variable = { congress_ruling_party_info = 5 }
			clear_parliament_gui_arrays = yes
			parliament_gui_initial = yes
			set_variable = { CongressPartyLeader = token:CongressPartyLeader_yi_won }
			set_variable = { CongressLeader = token:CongressLeader_park_chunghee_kks_bad }
			set_country_flag = FLAG_KOR_HYUKIL_SUCCESS
			set_power_balance = {
				id = KOR_balance
				left_side = KOR_the_emperor
				right_side = KOR_millitary
				set_default = yes 
				set_value = -0.65
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #독궈제국
	id = korea.10007
	title = korea.10007.title
	desc = korea.10007.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_777
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #
		name = korea.10007.a
		GER = {

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = korea.10007.b
		GER = {
			TLE_german_empire_lose = yes
		}	
	}
	option = { #항복
		name = korea.10007.c
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							tag = GER
						}
					}
					white_peace = POL
				}
				GER = {
					transfer_state = 85
					transfer_state = 807
					transfer_state = 86
					transfer_state = 762
					puppet = POL
				}
				POL = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = POL_KINGDOM
					promote_character = POL_karl_albrecht
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						HUN = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_EMPIRE
						}
					}
					HUN = {
						transfer_state = 987
						transfer_state = 88
						transfer_state = 91
						transfer_state = 89
						add_state_core = 987
						add_state_core = 88
						add_state_core = 91
						add_state_core = 89
					}
				}
	}	
	option = {
		name = korea.10007.d
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							tag = GER
						}
					}
					white_peace = LIT
				}
				GER = {
					transfer_state = 188
					puppet = LIT
				}
				LIT = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = LIT_KINGDOM
					add_ideas = { LIT_karl_gero_idea }
				}
	}	
	option = {
		name = korea.10007.e
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							tag = GER
						}
					}
					white_peace = CZE
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_country = {
							has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_EMPIRE
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_EMPIRE
						}
						annex_country = {
							target = CZE
							transfer_troops = no
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_country = {
								has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_EMPIRE
							}
						}
						GER = {
							owns_state = 4
						}
					}
					GER = {
						transfer_state = 69
						transfer_state = 74
						transfer_state = 72
						puppet = CZE
					}
					CZE = {
						set_cosmetic_tag = BOH_KINGDOM
						transfer_state = 9
						transfer_state = 75
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							HUN = {
								is_in_faction_with = GER
							}
						}
						HUN = {
							transfer_state = 70
							transfer_state = 71
							transfer_state = 73
							transfer_state = 664
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								HUN = {
									is_in_faction_with = GER
								}
							}
						}
						GER = {
							puppet = SLO
						}
						SLO = {
							transfer_state = 70
							transfer_state = 71
							transfer_state = 73

country_event = { #독궈제국
	id = korea.10011
	title = korea.10011.title
	desc = korea.10011.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_777
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #
		name = korea.10011.a
		set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
		KOR = {
			save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
		}
		JAP = {
			save_global_event_target_as = losing_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:losing_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:losing_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = losing_country_multiple
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:winning_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:winning_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = winning_country_multiple
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}	
			add_to_variable = { global.peace_popup_dirty = 1 }
		}
		log = "war_won"
		set_global_flag = war_won
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10011.b
		set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert

				}

			}

		}
		log = "war_won"
		set_global_flag = war_won
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10011.c
		set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert

			save_global_event_target_as = winning_country

				event_target:winning_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:winning_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = winning_country_multiple
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}	
			add_to_variable = { global.peace_popup_dirty = 1 }
		}
		log = "war_won"
		set_global_flag = war_won
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10012.d
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10012.e
	}
}
